DANG SER PO DANG DMAR PO'I ZHAL BZHIS MTSAN ZHING RIN PO CHE'I
DBU RGYAN DANG, COD PAN DU BCAS PA PHYAG G-YAS G-YON GYI DANG POS
RDO RJE RTZE LNGA PA THUGS KAR BSNYEMS PA'I TSUL DU GSOR ZHING
KHA tV'Am GA DRIL BU DANG BCAS PAS

'KHROL BA'O, ,'OG MA GNYIS MDA' DANG GZHU 'DZIN PA MTSAN BZANG PO
SUM CU RTZA GNYIS DANG DPE BYAD BZANG PO BRGYAD CUS SPRAS SHING
PHYAG RGYA LNGAS MDZES PA, ,SKU STOD DAR DKAR GSER GYI DANG RIS
STOD G-YOGS SU MNABS SHING SKU SMAD TSE GU'I NA BZA' CAN RIN PO
CHE'I PHRENG BA'I RKED CHINGS CAN

MGUR CHU DANG DO SHAL DANG, DPUNG RGYAN DANG PHYAG ZHABS KYI GDU
BU DANG, SE MO DOS MTSAN PA, ,RANG NYID KYI CHA 'DRA BA'AM, ,LHA
MO BDE MCHOG MA LTA BU'I KUN DU BZANG PO DANG ZHAL SBYOR DU
BZHUGS PA'O, ,DE'I PHYOGS BZHIR GSANG BA'I LHA MO BZHI RANG NYID
KYI CHA 'DRA BA'I 'OD KYI SKYES

BU BZHI LA 'KHRIL BA'I TSUL GYIS BZHUGS TE, SHAR DU LHA MO BDE
MCHOG MA SKU MDOG DKAR MO SNA TSOGS KYI GOS DANG RGYAN GYIS MDZES
PA, ,'GYING BAG GIS PHYAG NA MDA' GZHU 'GENGS PA STE PADMA'I
DKYIL 'KHOR LA GNAS PA'O, ,LHO PHYOGS SU AE MA BDE BA MO GSER GYI
MDOG

@314B CAN PHYAG NA BHA GA DANG LINGGA'I MTSAN MA 'DZIN CING RDO
RJE DANG RIN PO CHES BRGYAN PA'O, ,NUB PHYOGS SU LHA MO SNANG
MDZAD MA DMAR MDANGS CAN PHYAG G-YAS NA SNA TSOGS RDO RJE RGYA
GRAM 'DZIN CING BDAG PO'I SKU LA 'KHYUD NAS G-YON PAS THOD PA'I
SNOD BDUD RTZIS BKANG BA THOGS TE, KHA tV'Am GA GRU MOR

BCUG PA'O, ,BYANG PHYOGS SU SLOB MA MO AINDRA N'I LA'I MDOG CAN
G-YAS PAS BDAG PO LA 'KHYUD CING G-YON NA SANGS RGYAS KYI SKUS
MTSAN PA'I BDUD RTZI'I BUM PA BSNAMS PA'O, ,YANG PHYI ROL GYI
SHAR GYI RE'U MIG LA SANGS RGYAS KYI BYANG CHUB MA DKAR DMAR GYI
MDANGS CAN

TSANGS PA'I MGO BZHIS MTSAN PA'I MDA' BZHI DUS GCIG TU 'PHEN
PA'O, ,LHO PHYOGS SU CHOS KYI 'KHOR LO MA DKAR SER GYI MDANGS CAN
PHYAG G-YAS KYI GUR MO LA 'KHOR LO DKAR PO RTZIBS BRGYAD PA DANG,
SNGON PO RTZIBS BRGYAD PA GNYIS BRTZEGS PA'I TSUL DU BRGYUD CING

'DEBS PA'I TSUL GYIS BSTOD PA, ,G-YON PA 'GYING BAG GI TSUL GYIS
KHU TSUR DKU'I GNAS SU BRTEN TE BZHUGS PA'I, ,NUB PHYOGS SU KHAMS
GSUM RNAM RGYAL MA DMAR SKYA'I MDOG CAN G-YAS NA TRI SH'U LA RTZE
GSUM BSTOD PA'I TSUL CAN 'DZIN ZHING, G-YON PAS RDO RJE RTZE LNGA
PA

THUGS KAR BRTEN PA'O, ,BYANG PHYOGS SU 'DOD PA'I DBANG MO LJANG
GU'I MDOG CAN PHYAG GNYIS NA DPAG BSAM GYI SHING LCUG MA DANG
BCAS PA RLUNG GIS BSKYOD PA 'DZIN ZHING GAR MDZAD PA'O, ,DE LTAR
RTZA BA'I DKYIL 'KHOR GYI LHA MO DE DAG KUN KYANG RIN PO CHE'I
RGYAN DANG CHA BYAD KYIS

MDZES SHING, RANG 'OD KYI RIG MA DANG 'KHRIL BA'I TSUL GYIS ZHAL
SBYOR TE 'GYING BAG GI RNAM PAS BZHUGS PA'O, ,ME MTSAMS KYI RE'U
MIG LA RDO RJE GLING BU MA BEEd'URYA'I MDOG CAN RDO RJES MTSAN
PA'I GLING BU SGROGS PA'O, ,BDEN BRAL GYI RE'U MIG LA RDO RJE PI
WANG MA

GSER GYI MDOG CAN RDO RJES MTSAN PA'I PI WANG GLU DBYANGS KYI
DRUG GI SGRA SGROGS PA'O, ,RLUNG GI MTSAMS SU RDO RJE RNGA CHEN
MA AASMA R'A GA'I MDOG CAN RDO RJES MTSAN PA'I RNGA ZLUM BRDUNG
BA'O, ,DBANG LDAN GYI MTSAMS SU RDO RJE RDZA RNGA MA AINDRA N'I
LA'I MDOG CAN RDO RJES MTSAN PA'I RDZA RNGA

@315A *, ,BRDUNG BA'O, ,YANG PHYI ROL GYI ME MTSAMS SU RDO RJE ME
TOG MA DMAR MO RDO RJES MTSAN PA'I ME TOG GI GZHONG PA THOGS
PA'O, ,BDEN BRAL GYI MTSAMS SU RDO RJE SPOS ME MA DKAR SNGON RDO
RJE MTSAN PA'I SPOS ME THOGS PA'O, ,RLUNG GI MTSAMS SU RDO RJE ME
MA DMAR MO RDO RJES

MTSAN PA'I MAR ME 'DEGS PA'O, ,DBANG LDAN GYI MTSAMS SU RDO RJE
DRI CHAB MA LJANG GU RDO RJES MTSAN PA'I DRI CHAB 'THOR BA'O,
,YANG SHAR GYI SGOR RDO RJE RTA 'GRIN 'PHANG MTHO MA CHU SHEL GYI
MDOG CAN, G-YAS NA LCAGS KYU G-YON NA THOD PA'I BDUD RTZI RTA MGO
DANG BCAS PA'O, ,LHO PHYOGS KYI SGOR

PHAG GDONG MA BEEd'URYA'I MDOG CAN G-YAS NA MCHE BA G-YON NA
ZHAGS PA 'DZIN PA'O, ,NUB PHOGS KYI SGOR SNAG BA MO DMAR GSAL GYI
MDANGS CAN PHYAG GNYIS NA LCAGS SGROG NYI ZLAS MTSAN PA'O, ,BYANG
GYI SGRONG THAL BYED MA LHANG GU G-YAS NA DRIL BU 'KHROL ZHING,
G-YON PAS BHANDHA

BDUD RTZI'I NANG NAS SANGS RGYAS SNANG BA MTHA' YAS KYI SKU
PHYUNG BA'O, ,LHA MO NYI SHU PO DE DAG KYANG RGYAN DANG CHA LUGS
DANG 'OD KYI DKYIL 'KHOR GYIS MDZES PAR GYUR RO, ,BSDUS PA'I
DBANG DU NI LHA MO KUN KYANG KHA DOG 'DRA BAR LE'U DGU PA LAS
GSUNGS PA'I DON BZHIN BSTAN PA'O, ,YANG RNAM PAR

SNANG MDZAD KYI DKYIL 'KHOR GYI RNAM PAR 'PHRUL BA'I PHYIR, ,RDO
RJE 'CHANG CHEN PO NYID LAS SNANG BA'I SANGS RGYAS DE NYID GSER
GYI MDOG CAN NYI MA 'BUM GYI 'OD DANG LDAN PA'I GANGS RI'I LHUN
PO LTAR BZHUGS PA, ,GSER DANG KA RTI KA DANG, AINDRA N'I LA DANG
AASMA R'A GA'I MDOG CAN GYI ZHAL BZHI DANG LNGA PA, PHYAG BZHI

NA CHOS GOS DANG LHUNG BZED DANG 'KHAR SIL DANG, DAM PA'I CHOS
KYI GLEGS BAM 'DZIN PA'I 'KHOR LOS SGYUR BA'I RGYAL PO'I CHA LUGS
CAN RIN PO CHE SNA BDUN DANG 'DOD PA'I LONGS SPYOD KUN GYIS NYE
BAR MDZES PA, ,RANG 'OD KYI RIG MA YUM SANGS RGYAS SPYAN MA DANG
NYIS SU MED PAR ZHAL SBYOR GYI TSUL DU

BZHUGS PA'O, ,DE NYID KYI SHAR DU SANGS RGYAS KUN BRJOD MA CHU
SHES KYI MDOG CAN RIN PO CHE'I RGYAN KUN GYIS MDZES PAR BYAS PA,
,PHAG NA ME LCES MTSAN PA'I PADMA 'DZIN PA'O, ,LHO PHYOGS SU DPA'
MO SHIN TU RGYAL MA GSER GYI MDOG CAN PHYAG GNYIS NA CHA LANG
'DZIN PA'O, ,NUB PHYOGS NA KUN TU BZANG MO

@315B PADMA R'A GA'I MDOG CAN PHYAG GNYIS NA RDO RJE RTZE LNGA PA
DANG RIN PO CHE'I ZA MA TOG 'DZIN PA'O, ,BYANG PHYOGS NA MI BZANG
RIN PO CHE'I SNOD 'DZIN MA, ,SNA TSOGS KYI MDOG CAN RIN PO CHES
BKANG BA'I SNOD DANG CHOS KYI DUNG 'DZIN PA'O, ,YANG PHYI ROL GYI
SHAR PHYOGS KYI RE'U CHA LA SANGS RGYAS KUN 'DZIN MA GUR GUM

GYI MDOG CAN SANGS RGYAS MI BSKYOD PA'I SKU THUGS KAR 'DZIN PA'O,
,LHO PHYOGS NA LHA MO ZHAL BZANGS MA ME LONG GI MDOG CAN PHYAG
GNYIS ME LONG DANG RNGA YAB 'DZIN PA'O, ,NUB PHYOGS SU LHA MO
SPRIN CHEN MA BEEd'URYA'I MDOG CAN PHYAG GNYIS KYIS RDO RJE SPRIN
GYI DKYIL 'KHOR LAS SER BA 'BEBS PA'O, ,BYANG

PHYOGS SU NAM MKHA'I SPYAN MA SER SKYA'I MDOG CAN PHYAG GNYIS

BZHI DANG, RTA MGRIN 'PHANG MTHO MA LA SOGS PA BZHI PO DAG NI,

'KHOR LAS BSTAN PA DANG 'DRA BAR GNAS PA LAS, ,CUNG ZIG GI KHYAD
PAR NI ZHI BA'I CHA LUGS 'DZIN CING RGYAN DANG PHYAG MTSAN LA
'KHOR LO'I RNAM PAS MTSAN PA'O, ,YANG DPAL HE DU KA'I DKYIL 'KHOR
RNAM PAR 'PHRUL BA'I PHYIR RDO RJE 'CHANG CHEN PO NYID LAS SNAG
BA'I 'BRAS BU'I HE RU KA DE NYID SKU

BEEd'URYA'I MDOG CAN 'BAR BA CHEN PO'I 'OD ZER DANG BCAS PA,

CHA LUGS CAN, RGYAB MA CHAGS 'DZAD DMAR PO'I ZHAL G-YON PA RMONGS
MDZAD SER POR BZHUGS PA, SMIN MTSAMS KYI KHRO GNYER BU 'GYUR
ZHING SPYAN MIG DMAR PO

LAS 'JIGS PA'I ME STAG 'PHRO BA DANG, ,DBU SKRA DANG SMAR SER NAG
TU 'KHYIL ZHING GYEN DU BRDZES PA BA SPU RNAMS RDO RJE'I TSUL
GYIS G-YAS SU 'KHYIL PA ZHAL GDANGS PA DANG, MCHE BA GTZIGS PA
DANG, LJAGS 'DRIL BA DANG, RKAN BRDAB PA DANG, 'DZUM PA'I MDANGS
KYIS GNAS PA DANG,

SGEG PA DANG, DPA' BA DANG, 'JIGS SU RUNG BA DANG, DGOD PA DANG,
GSHE BA DANG, 'JIGS PAR BYED PA DANG, SNYING RJE DANG, RNGAM PA
DANG, ZHI BA'I MDANGS KYIS GNAS PA, PHYAG G-YAS G-YON GYI DANG PO
NA RDO RJE DANG, RDO RJE KHA tV'Am GA DRIL BUS MTSAN PA 'DZIN PA,
,DE'I 'OG MA GNYIS KYIS 'JIGS BYED

@316A *, ,CHEN PO'I PAGS PA RLUNG GI TSUL GYIS BSKOR BA, GSUM PA
GNYIS NA MDA' DANG GZHU 'DZIN PA, G-YAS KYI BZHI PA NA DUNG CHEN
PO KHRAG GIS BKANG ZHING GSOL BA'I STABS KYIS GNAS PA, G-YON GYI
BZHI PA NA DUNG CHEN PO SNYING GIS BKANG BA'O, ,YANG LA LAR ZHAL
GCIG PHYAG BZHI

PA LA G-YAS GNYIS RDO RJE DANG DUNG KHRAG GIS BKANG BA, G-YON

RAL KHAR THOGS PA'O, ,YANG LA LAR ZHAL GCIG PHYAG GNYIS PA LA RDO
RJE DANG DUNG CHEN PO KHRAG GIS BKANG PA 'DZIN CING, ,KHA tV'Am

SKU LA GLANG CHEN GYI KO RLON DANG, SPRUL GYI CHUN PO DANG, STAG

BZHUGS PA'O, ,DE NYID KYI MDUN GYI SHAR PHYOGS SU GOO R'I DKAR
SER ZHI BA'I MDANGS CAN, ZHAL BZHI PHYAG BRGYAD NA MDA' DANG GZHU
'GENGS PA LAS TSANGS PA'I MGO BO BZHI SBYANGS PA G-YON BRKYANG

DRAG PO'I MDANGS CAN G-YON NA

'GYUR BA'I BZHIN DANG BCAS

PO DANG, ZHI BA'I SGO NAS GZIGS PA'I MDANGS CAN RIN PO CHE SNA
TSOGS KYI RGYAN DANG, KHYAD PAR GYI RTAGS KYIS RNAM PAR SPRAS
PA'O, ,G-YAS PHYOGS SU SNA TSOGS PADMO LJANG SER

GYI SKU LAS 'OD ZER 'PHROS PA PHYAG NA SNA TSOGS PADMA 'DZIN
PA'O, ,G-YON PHYOGS SU SNA TSOGS RDO RJE MA SKU MDOG LJANG SNGON
LAS 'OD ZER 'PHRO BA, PHYAG NA SNA TSOGS RDO RJE 'DZIN PA'O,
,MDUN DU RANG 'OD KYI SNANG BA YUM DAM TSIG SGROL MA DANG ZHAL
SBYOR GYI TSUL DU 'KHRIL NAS BZHUGS PA'O, ,'KHOR GYI LHA MO

GZHAN DAG NI PHRIN LAS KYI BYE BRAG BZHIN DU, RIGS KYI DKYIL
'KHOR GZHAN DAG GI LHA MO DANG MTHUN PA LAS, CUNG ZHIG MI 'DRA
BA'I KHYAD PAR DU NI SKU DANG, PHYAG MTSAN DAG LA SNA TSOGS RDO
RJES MTSAN CING DBU LA DON YOD GRUB PA'I SKUS BRGYAN PA'O, ,LHA
MO GZHAN DAG GIS DKYIL 'KHOR GYI GTZO

BO MDZAD PA'I 'KHOR LO MI 'DRA BA DAG DANG, RIGS BSDUS KYI DKYIL
'KHOR GYI 'JIG RTEN PA'I LHA SNA TSOGS RNAMS NI GDUL BYA'I MOS PA
BZHIN DU BYUNG ZHING, MGRON THABS SU BKOD DE PHRIN LAS KYI PHYAG
BRNYAN PA YIN PAS DKYIL 'KHOR GYI GRANGS SU BZHAG KYANG, SKABS
'DIR SPRUL PA'I LHA MA YIN

PA'I PHYIR BSHAD PAR MI BYA STE RJES SU 'JUG PA'I SGRUB PA BOS
SGRUB PA'I DUS SU NI TSOGS KYI 'KHOR LO'I SGRUB THABS LAS RGYA
CHER BSTAN PA BZHIN DU SHES PAR BYA'O, ,DA NI LHA DE DAG GI
BZHUGS THABS BSTAN PA'I PHYIR, STAN DE DAG NI THAMS CAD LA JI
LTAR GNAS PA BZHIN DU DGOD, DPAL RDO RJE SEMS

DPA'I DKYIL 'KHOR GYI LHA RNAMS NI ZHABS G-YAS G-YON GYI SBYOR
BAS BDE BA'I CHA LUGS BZHIN DU GAR BYED CING SEMS DPA'I SKYIL MO
KRUNG DU BZHUGS PA'O, ,SANGS RGYAS RNAM PAR SNANG MDZAD KYI RIGS
KYI LHA RNAMS NI G-YAS PA'I YAN LAG GNON PAS G-YON PA'I YAN LAG
KUN LAS RGYAS TE

SEMS DPA'I 'GYING TSUL GYIS BZHUGS PA'O, ,RDO RJE HE RU KA'I LHA
RNAMS NI G-YAS G-YON GYI SBYOR BAS BDE BA'I GAR BYED CING SKYIL
MO KRUNG PHYED PA'I TSUL DU RKANG PA RANG GI BRLAS MNAN PA'O,
,PADMA GAR DBANG GI LHA RNAMS NI G-YAS G-YON GYI SBYOR BAS SKYIL
KRUNG PHYED PA'I TSUL DU RGYAL PO'I

@318B SKYIL KRUNG GIS GNAS PA'O, ,RDO RJE NYI MA'I LHA RNAMS NI
PUS MO GNYIS GSHIBS TE RDO RJE'I SKYIL KRUNG GIS BZHUGS PA'O,
,RTA MCHOG GI LHA RNAMS G-YAS G-YON GYI SBYOR BAS BRKYANG BSKUM
GYI TSUL GYIS KHRO BO'I SKYIL MO KRUNG BCINGS PA'O, ,DE DAG THAMS
CAD KYANG GDAN PADMA'I DKYIL 'KHOR LA RANG

RANG GI CHA LUGS KYIS DANG MTSAN NYID KYIS GNAS PA'O, ,DE LTAR
BRTEN PA'I LHA'I DKYIL 'KHOR RNAMS KYI BZHUGS GNAS LHA'I GZHAL
YAS KHANG JI LTA BU ZHE NA, GRU BZHI PA LA SGO BZHI PA, ,RTA BABS
BZHI YIS MDZES PAR BYAS, ,RDO RJE RIN CHEN PADMO SOGS, ,SGO SRUNG
DANG NI LDAN PAR BYA, ,PHYI ROL GYI

RGYAR NI RA BA RIM PA GSUM DANG BCAS PA'I DUR KHROD BRGYAD KYIS
BRGYAN CING, DE'I NANG DU GZHAL YAS KHANG GRU BZHI PA LA SGO BZHI
PA SANGS RGYAS KYI CHE BA'I YON TAN THAMS CAD KYIS RGYAS SHING
TSAD MED PA BZHI LA SBYANGS PAS RNAM PAR THAR BA'I SGO BZHIR 'JUG
PA, BYANG CHUB KYI PHYOGS KYI CHOS SUM CU RTZA

BDUN LA SOGS PAS MTSON PA'I MTSAN MA RTA BABS LA SOGS PA'I RGYAN
DANG, RIGS KYI MTSAN MAS RANG NYID KYI YE SHES YON TAN GYI TSOGS
DANG BCAS PA'I RTAGS MTSON PA RANG GI RIGS KYI SGO SRUNG DANG
LDAN PA'O, ,DE YANG RTZA BA'I RGYUD LAS, GSER GYI 'KHOR LO SNA
TSOGS RDO RJE'I DBUS, ,GRU

BZHI SGO KHYUD RTA BABS BZHI YIS MTSAN, ,RIN CHEN SNA LNGA'I
PHYOGS KYI RTZIG PA LA, ,RANG BYUNG NYI SHU LNGA YI 'OD DANG
BCAS, ,RDO RJES MTSAN PA'I KA BA MCHOG BRGYAD SPRAS, ,RIN CHEN MU
TIG ME TOG PHRENG BAS MDZES, ,GZUGS SGRA DRI RO REG BYA'I LHA MO
'KHRIGS, ,GDUGS DANG RGYAL MTSAN BLA

RE RNGA YAB DANG, ,ZLA PHYED RDO RJE RIN CHEN BA DAN BCAS, ,DRIL
BU SNYAN PA'I SGRA SOGS THAMS CAD SGROGS, ,ZHES SO, ,DE NYID KYIS
NANG GI PHO BRANG NI RIGS BSDUS KYI DKYIL 'KHOR DANG, RIGS SO SO
DAG GI DKYIL 'KHOR GYI BYE BRAG GIS SHES PAR BYA'O, ,DE NYID DU
LHA'I RTEN GYI DKYIL 'KHOR

DGOD PA'I PHYIR, RANG GI LHA DANG 'DRA BA YI, ,BUD MED DAG NI
LEGS BSGRUB PA, ,SKAL BZANG RANG GI PHYAG RGYAS MTSAN, ,TSOGS KYI
DKYIL 'KHOR BRTAG PAR BYA, ,RIGS SO SO'I DKYIL 'KHOR GYI TSUL
GYIS LHA MO RANG GI RTAGS DANG KHA DOG DANG MTSAN MAS BRGYAN
CING, RANG RANG GI

@319A *, ,TING NGE 'DZIN LA GNAS TE DE NYID KYI SKU LEGS PAR
BSGRUBS NAS, RANG RANG GI PHYOGS SU SKAL PA BZANG PO'I DAM TSIG
LAS BYUNG BA'I PHYAG RGYA'I TSUL GYIS GNAS PAR BYA'O, ,DE LTAR
PHYAG RGYA BZHI DANG LDAN PA'I SGO NAS SPRO BA DANG BSDU BA'I RIM
PAS YON TAN GYI SNANG BA THAMS CAD SKAD CIG

LA RDZOGS PAR BYA BA'I PHYIR TSOGS KYI DKYIL 'KHOR BRTAG PAR
BYA'O, ,GA NA BINDHU RA ZHES PAS SKAL LDAN DANG 'BYOR LDAN GYI
PHUN SUM TSOGS PA THAMS CAD 'DUS PAR BSHAD DO, ,GHA NA BI HA RA
ZHES PAS DE NYID LA SPYOD PAS DE LTA BU'I RTAGS GSAL ZHING, YUN
RING DU BRTAGS PAS DE DANG MTHUN

PA'I 'BRAS BU 'GRUB PA'O, ,DA NI RNAL 'BYOR BAS TSOGS KYI DBUS SU
BDUD RTZI LNGA BSGRUB PA'I PHYIR, ME YI TSAL NI GRUB PA LA, ,DMAR
CHEN PO ZHES BYA BAR BSHAD, ,CES PA LA SOGS PA'I TSIGS SU BCAD PA
DRUG GSUNGS TE, GANG ZHIG RANG GI TING NGE 'DZIN GSAL BAR BYA BA
DANG, DNGOS

GRUB KYI RDZAS KHYAD PAR CAN LA BRTEN NAS 'DOD PA'I DON SGRUB
PA'I PHYIR BDUD RTZI LNGA GROGS DANG BCAS PA LAS, BSNYEN SGRUB
KYI YAN LAG GIS SGRUB PA'I THABS BSTAN TE, DE YANG TSIGS SU BCAD
PA DANG POS NI SNGAGS KYIS DRANGS PA'I MTSAL CHEN PO DAG NI,
SGRON MA GNYIS KYI RTEN DU GYUR PAS RANG GI

SGRA DANG LDAN TE DE LA BRTEN NAS SGRA'I DNGOS GRUB NGO BO NYID
KYI MTHU DANG RANG BZHIN GYIS GRUB PA DAG GSAL BAR BYA BA DANG,
TSIGS SU BCAD PA GNYIS PAS RDO RJE DANG CHU DANG RDO RJE DRI CHEN
DANG, MTSAL CHEN PO DANG SBYAR ZHING BSGRUBS TE PADMA'I SNOD DU
BZHAG NAS, THUGS YE SHES RNAM PA LNGA'I RTAGS BLTA BA

DANG; TSIGS SU BCAD PA GSUM PAS DE NYID KYI MTSAN MA GSAL BAR
GRUB PA'I YON TAN BSHAD CING DE LAS MI 'DA' BAR GNAS PA DANG,
TSIGS SU BCAD PA BZHI PAS DE NYID KYI MTSAN NYID NGES TSIG DANG
BCAS PAR BSTAN PA, TSIGS SU BCAD PA LNGA BAS NI BDUD RTZI LNGA LA
SBYOR BA'I DNGOS

GRUB KYI DRIL BU SGRUB PA'I THABS DANG, DE'I PHAN YON BSTAN TO,
,TSIGS SU BCAD PA DRUG PAS NI DNGOS GRUB DE DAG GI NYAMS SU BLANG
BA'I CHO GA 'BRAS BU DANG BCAS PA STE, BRAM ZE RNAMS KYI NYI MA
DANG, ZLA BA'I MCHOD SBYIN CHEN PO BYED PA'I DUS SU, ,BRANGGA
RA'I RGYAL PO'I BRDA SBYOR BSHAMS PA

@319B BZHIN DU DA DU RA'I G-YOS BSHAMS PA MYANG BA LTAR BTUNG BA

GSUM DU BLANGS PA DANG, SKU GSUNG THUGS RTAG PA'I DNGOS GRUB SKYE

DU 'GYUR RO, ,BDUD RTZI DE NYID KYI BSRUNG BA'I CHO GA NI, 'DIS

LES DBANG PO LNGA LA

THIG LE BYA ZHING, BSRUNG BA BYAS PAS DE NYID DU RIGS RNAM PA

'THUNGS SHING GNAS GSUM DU YANG BYUGS PAS DPAL RDO RJE SEMS DPA'

YIS; ,GNAS RNAMS KUN DU BRGYAN BYAS PAS, ,DE NYID RIGS KYI DKYIL

PA MANG BAS MA BSHAD DO, ,DE LTAR BSOD NAMS KYI TSOGS BSAGS NAS

BGOS NAS NI, ,ME TOG PHRENG LDAN KHA DRI ZHIM, ,PHYI NANG GSANG

ZHUGS NAS, DE BZHIN DU NI YON PHUL TE, GSANG BA'I CHO GA NYID
SHES PAS MI 'GYUR BA'I MCHOG

'GRUB PA'O, ,SLOB MA YOL BA'I NANG DU BCUG NAS CHO GA RNAM PA
LNGA RDZOGS PAR BYAS PA'I RJES SU SKU GSUNG THUGS KYI RDO RJE
SBYIN ZHING, YE SHES DBAB PA'I CHO GA RNAM PA LNGA DANG, 'JUG
PA'I CHO GA LNGAS RDZOGS PAR BYAS TE, RJES SU BYA BA'I LAS MIG
DBYE BA DANG, GDONG G-YOGS BSAL

ZHING DKYIL 'KHOR BLTA BA DANG, YON PHUL BA DANG, BKA' BSGO BA
DAG BYA'O, ,DES NI GSANG BA'I CHO GA NYID SHES NAS DE'I DON BZHIN
DU 'JUG CING SPYOD PAS MI 'GYUR BA'I MCHOG 'GRUB PA'O, ,DE LA YON
GYI RIM PA NI, KUN DU SNA TSOGS BLA MA LA, ,YON MCHOG DAG NI DBUL
BAR NGES, ,

ZHES PA LA SOGS PA'I TSIGS SU BCAD PA DGU GSUNGS TE, DANG POR
DPAL RDO RJE SEMS DPA' DANG, RDO RJE SLOB DPON GNYIS SU MED PA'I
TSUL DU GNAS PA DAG MNYES PAR BYA BA YIN NO, ,GANG RANG LA PHANGS
SHING SHIN TU GTONG BAR DKA' BA'I RNAM PA DAG DANG, RANG GI
SNYING DU SDUG PA DAG

DANG; KHYAD PAR CAN GYI RDZAS KYI RNAM PA DAG GIS MNYES PAR

KHYAD PAR 'DRA BA LAS PHAN PA'I SGO NAS

ZHING MI 'DOD PA'I 'BRAS BU NYAMS

,GSANG SNGAGS RGYUD

KYI SBYOR BA SHES, ,DKYIL 'KHOR GYI NI LAS LA BRTZON, ,SEMS CAN

TU BRTAG DKA' MUN KHAMS 'OD KYI RIN CHEN GZUGS, ,DU MA'I RTOG
BCOM CHO GA KUN STON

@389A *, ,PA; ;BDE CHEN PHYAG RGYA NGO MTSAR RMAD DU BYUNG,
,SKYABS MDZAD THUGS GNYIS NYI ZER RIM SHAR 'DRA, ,BLO YI MUN SEL
RIN CHEN ZUR MANG GSAL, ,LEGS BSHAD TSUL MANG MKHAS PA'I SPYOD
YUL YIN, ,RNAM PAR BSHAD LAS 'GAL MED RMAD DU

BYUNG; ;PHYI DUS RTOG MANG BLO GROS MTHA' YAS RNAMS, ,LEGS BSHAD
RGYAL BA'I GSUNG LA'ANG MGU DKA' BA, ,BDAG LA BRTEN TE SGRO SKUR
SMOD 'DZUGS 'GYUR, ,DE DAG SGRIB BSAGS DRI MA DAG GYUR CIG ,RDUL
BRAL GANGS RI RIN CHEN LHUN PO'I RGYAN, ,SKAR

TSOGS ZLA RGYAS NYI MA'I 'OD MDANGS KYIS, ,MI MTHUN PHYOGS BRAL
LEGS PA'I LAM ZHUGS TE, ,MTSUNGS MED 'KHOR LOS SGYUR RGYAL GNAS
THOB SHOG ,DPAL SANGS RGYAS THAMS CAD DANG MNYAM PAR SBYOR BA
MKHA' 'GRO SGYU MA'I MCHOG GI DON RNAM PAR BSHAD

PA ZHES BYA BA, DPAL AU RGYAN GYI MKHAS PA CHEN PO 'DZAM BU GLING
GI NYI MA DANG 'DRA BA, DNGOS GRUB THOB PA'I SLOB DPON RGYAL PO
CHEN PO BRGYA BYIN SDONG POS MDZAD PA RDZOGS SO,, ,,RGYA GAR GYI
MKHAN PO BIDY'A KA RA SIm HA DANG, ZHU CHEN GYI LO TZ'A BA BANDE

LHA'I RIN PO CHES BSGYUR CING ZHUS TE, SKAD GSAR CHAD KYIS PHYIS
LEGS PAR GTAN LA PHAB PA,,
